#extension GL_OES_EGL_image_external : require
#define mediump
#define highp
#define lowp
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION
#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
#else
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
#endif
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
precision mediump float;
uniform mat4 u_projection;
attribute vec2 a_position;
attribute vec4 a_color;
attribute vec2 a_texCoord;
varying vec2 v_texCoord;
varying vec4 v_color;
void main()
    v_texCoord = a_texCoord;
    gl_Position = u_projection * vec4(a_position, 0.0, 1.0);
    gl_PointSize = 1.0;
    v_color = a_color;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(0, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1,       1,        1,
                          0,      -0.3441,   1.772,
                          1.402,  -0.7141,   0);
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb = matrix * yuv;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(-0.0627451017, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1.1644,  1.1644,   1.1644,
                          0,      -0.3918,   2.0172,
                          1.596,  -0.813,    0);
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb = matrix * yuv;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(-0.0627451017, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1.1644,  1.1644,   1.1644,
                          0,      -0.2132,   2.1124,
                          1.7927, -0.5329,   0);
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb = matrix * yuv;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(0, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1,       1,        1,
                          0,      -0.3441,   1.772,
                          1.402,  -0.7141,   0);
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).ra;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb = matrix * yuv;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(-0.0627451017, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1.1644,  1.1644,   1.1644,
                          0,      -0.3918,   2.0172,
                          1.596,  -0.813,    0);

    vec3 yuv, rgb;
    // Get the Y value 
    tcoord = v_texCoord;
    yuv.x = texture2D(tex0, tcoord).r;
    // Get the U and V values 
    tcoord *= UVCoordScale;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(tex1, tcoord).ar;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb.r = dot(yuv, Rcoeff);
    rgb.g = dot(yuv, Gcoeff);
    rgb.b = dot(yuv, Bcoeff);
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1.0) * v_color;

#extension GL_OES_EGL_image_external : require
#define mediump
#define highp
#define lowp
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION
#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
#else
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
#endif
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
precision mediump float;
uniform mat4 u_projection;
attribute vec2 a_position;
attribute vec4 a_color;
attribute vec2 a_texCoord;
varying vec2 v_texCoord;
varying vec4 v_color;
void main()
    v_texCoord = a_texCoord;
    gl_Position = u_projection * vec4(a_position, 0.0, 1.0);
    gl_PointSize = 1.0;
    v_color = a_color;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(0, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1,       1,        1,
                          0,      -0.3441,   1.772,
                          1.402,  -0.7141,   0);
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb = matrix * yuv;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(-0.0627451017, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1.1644,  1.1644,   1.1644,
                          0,      -0.3918,   2.0172,
                          1.596,  -0.813,    0);
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb = matrix * yuv;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;

                          1.7927, -0.5329,   0);

const vec3 offset = vec3(0, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1,       1,        1,
                          0,      -0.3441,   1.772,
                          1.402,  -0.7141,   0);
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).ar;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb = matrix * yuv;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;

uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;

'PSU
#extension GL_OES_EGL_image_external : require
#define mediump
#define highp
#define lowp
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION
#ifdef GL_FRAGMENT_PRECISION_HIGH
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
#else
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
#endif
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION mediump
precision mediump float;
#define SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION highp
precision mediump float;
uniform mat4 u_projection;
attribute vec2 a_position;
attribute vec4 a_color;
attribute vec2 a_texCoord;
varying vec2 v_texCoord;
varying vec4 v_color;
void main()
    v_texCoord = a_texCoord;
    gl_Position = u_projection * vec4(a_position, 0.0, 1.0);
    gl_PointSize = 1.0;
    v_color = a_color;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    gl_FragColor = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.r = abgr.b;
    gl_FragColor.b = abgr.r;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
void main()
    mediump vec4 abgr = texture2D(u_texture, v_texCoord);
    gl_FragColor = abgr;
    gl_FragColor.a = 1.0;
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(0, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1,       1,        1,
                          0,      -0.3441,   1.772,
                          1.402,  -0.7141,   0);
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb = matrix * yuv;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;
uniform sampler2D u_texture;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;
varying mediump vec4 v_color;
varying SDL_TEXCOORD_PRECISION vec2 v_texCoord;
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(-0.0627451017, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const mat3 matrix = mat3( 1.1644,  1.1644,   1.1644,
                          0,      -0.3918,   2.0172,
                          1.596,  -0.813,    0);
void main()
    mediump vec3 yuv;
    lowp vec3 rgb;
    // Get the YUV values 
    yuv.x = texture2D(u_texture,   v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.y = texture2D(u_texture_u, v_texCoord).r;
    yuv.z = texture2D(u_texture_v, v_texCoord).r;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb = matrix * yuv;
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1);
    gl_FragColor *= v_color;

uniform sampler2D u_texture_u;
uniform sampler2D u_texture_v;

const vec3 offset = vec3(-0.0627451017, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);
// RGB coefficients 
const vec3 Rcoeff = vec3(1.1644,  0.000,  1.7927);
const vec3 Gcoeff = vec3(1.1644, -0.2132, -0.5329);
const vec3 Bcoeff = vec3(1.1644,  2.1124,  0.000);
void main()
    vec2 tcoord;
    vec3 yuv, rgb;
    // Get the Y value 
    tcoord = v_texCoord;
    yuv.x = texture2D(tex0, tcoord).r;
    // Get the U and V values 
    tcoord *= UVCoordScale;
    yuv.yz = texture2D(tex1, tcoord).rg;
    // Do the color transform 
    yuv += offset;
    rgb.r = dot(yuv, Rcoeff);
    rgb.g = dot(yuv, Gcoeff);
    rgb.b = dot(yuv, Bcoeff);
    // That was easy. :) 
    gl_FragColor = vec4(rgb, 1.0) * v_color;
varying vec4 v_color;
varying vec2 v_texCoord;
uniform sampler2D tex0; // Y 
uniform sampler2D tex1; // U/V 
// YUV offset 
const vec3 offset = vec3(0, -0.501960814, -0.501960814);

const vec3 Gcoeff = vec3(1, -0.3441, -0.7141);
const vec3 Bcoeff = vec3(1,  1.772,  0.000);

    vec2 tcoord;
